msg:The hotel is 2 stops away from the south gate of the scenic area, 10 minutes by free bus, and 3 minutes by car. The hotel environment is very good, with its own courtyard. It is one of the few five-star hotels nearby. There are two types of rooms: villa rooms and main buildings. The villa rooms have 4-5 rooms on each floor, all with balconies. There are chess and card tables and tea sets in the public area, which are suitable for family groups to travel. The main building is a standard hotel room. You can see the mountain view in the direction of the mountain. The picture is taken in the room. The environment is very good, the hotel service is standardized, and the attitude is also very good. There are many types of breakfast, including milk, coffee, bread, and Chinese food. The noodles are freshly made, and the noodles are not so good. The vegetables and seafood are relatively fresh. There are also many seats, and there is basically no need to wait for a seat when there are many people on holidays.
